/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[GetList]    Script Date: 2017/12/10 15:21:28 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create proc [dbo].[GetList]

 @str nvarchar(50),
 @floor int,
 @roomNumber nvarchar(10),
 @time nvarchar(20)
 as
 begin
 DECLARE @sql  nvarchar(500)
 set @sql=
  'select  Rn_roomNum  FROM room_number as a 
  inner join( 
  select room_number from occu_infor as oi inner join 
  (select SUM(ga_price)-SUM(ga_sum_price) 
  as sa,ga_occuid as t from goods_account 
  where ga_isys=1  group by ga_occuid) 
  as u on u.t =oi.order_id 
  where  '+@str+' u.sa>0 and datediff(D,[depar_time],'''+@time+''')=0) 
  as uio on uio.room_number=a.Rn_roomNum and  Rn_floor='+CAST( @floor AS VARCHAR(50)) +' and room_number='''+ @roomNumber +''''
  exec (@sql)
 end
GO
